  • Make monthly river forcing files for 1998–2018
  • Included Datasets
    • CIRCAC: Central Cook Inlet Mooring
    • KBNERR: Lower Cook Inlet Mooring
    • NOAA: Single CTD profiles across Cook Inlet
    • CMI KBNERR: Six repeat transects, one single transect, and one time series of CTD profiles in Cook Inlet
    • CMI UAF: CTD transect from East Foreland Lighthouse in Cook Inlet
    • GWA: Six repeat transects in Cook Inlet
    • OTF KBNERR: Repeat CTD transect from Anchor Point in Cook Inlet
    • USGS BOEM: Single CTD profiles across Cook Inlet
    • UAF: Repeat CTD profile transect along an east-west section in central Cook Inlet
    • NOAA PMEL: Towed CTD on ferry at nominal 4m depth
    • GWA: Towed CTD at nominal 7m depth
    • OTF KBNERR: Short, high resolution towed CTD in the middle of Cook Inlet at nominal 4 and 10m depths
    • CDIP Buoys: Lower Cook Inlet, Kodiak, Central Cook Inlet
    • KBNERR Moorings: Kachemak Bay
    • Historical KBNERR Moorings: Kachemak Bay
    • NOAA Moorings: Geese Island, Sitkalidak Island, Bear Cove, Anchorage, Kodiak Island, Alitak, Seldovia, Old Harbor, Boulder Point, Albatross Banks, Shelikof Strait
    • NPS Moorings: Chinitna Bay and Aguchik Island, Cook Inlet
    • UAF Moorings: Kodiak Island and Peterson Bay, Cook Inlet
    • GWA: Towed CTD at nominal 7m depth, temperature only

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

from ciofs_hindcast_report.src.create_river_roms import *
import ciofs_hindcast_report as chr

import os
from IPython.display import Code

plt.rc('font', size=16)

Make monthly river forcing files for 1998–2018#

base = chr.PATH_OUTPUTS_RIVER

def run_year(year):
    
        start, end = f"{year}-1-1T00", f"{year+1}-1-1T00"

        fname = pd.Timestamp(start).strftime("axiom.ciofs.river.%Y%m%d.nc")
        fname = f"{base}/{fname}"
        
        if not os.path.exists(fname) or not os.path.exists(fname.replace(".nc",".txt")):
            ds = create_river_forcing_file(start, end, ndays=7, skip_last=False)
            ds.to_netcdf(fname)
        
        print(Code(fname.replace(".nc",".txt")))

        
def plot_year(year):
    locs = f"{base}/axiom.ciofs.river.{year}*.nc"
    ds = xr.open_mfdataset(locs, concat_dim="time", combine='nested')
    ds = ds.swap_dims({"time": "river_time"})

    unique_inds = list(set([station_list_file.index(station_list_file[i]) for i in range(nrivers)]))
    labels = [station_list_file[i] for i in unique_inds]
    nrepeats = [station_list_file.count(station) for station in labels]
    abs(ds["river_transport"].isel(river=unique_inds)*nrepeats).plot.line(x="river_time", lw=3, figsize=(15,7));
    plt.legend(labels)

    ds["river_temp"].isel(s_rho=0, river=unique_inds).plot.line(x="river_time", lw=3, figsize=(15,7));
    plt.legend(labels)

1998#

year = 1998
run_year(year)
